/-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------/

			NETFLOW WORKING RULES WITH MANY ATTRIBUTES 

/-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------/
(1) there is no attribute IP flags in netflow, but TCP FLAGS is there so protocol is TCP.(we assume protocol is TCP for IP protocol )
(2) there is no attribtue ID in netflow related to IP protocol,but FLOW_SAMPLER_ID exists .(we assume protocol is TCP for IP protocol )
(3) there is no attribute ID  in netflow for ICMP but ICMP_IPv4_CODE exists.(we assume protocol is TCP for IP protocol )
(4) there is no attribute UNUSED and SEQ in netflow for ICMP but ICMP_IPv4_TYPE exists.(we assume protocol is TCP for IP protocol )
(5) there is no attribute CHKSUM in netflow for TCP and IP protocol but FORWARDING_STATUS exists(we assume protocol is TCP for IP protocol ).

/-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------/
